	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '3242a8c00e2d99bad1ed562fd3a006dff7895e8c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3242a8c00e2d99bad1ed562fd3a006dff7895e8c') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ed1456887b83c4df838fa8b2234def3a9a3f4861') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3242a8c00e2d99bad1ed562fd3a006dff7895e8c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '2e185e9bb3bb6890fc2abc32451c127375024e2a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2e185e9bb3bb6890fc2abc32451c127375024e2a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '68926cdca6b92b073599a109ceba1bf8d10eb9ed') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2e185e9bb3bb6890fc2abc32451c127375024e2a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') != 'bbe4b7b57ec115f6f0ca5060d4b3a5c6431a6bca') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') !== 'bbe4b7b57ec115f6f0ca5060d4b3a5c6431a6bca') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

				warn('Creation of backup failed');
